Pae V
T e Moni a te Iti tangata Kuki Airani
67 Moni a te Iti tangata
E Akunı ¯ti ta te Kavamani Kuki Airani ka akatupu ia takake mei te moni a te
katoatoa me kore au akunı ¯ti ka akataka ia e te ture.
68 Kotinga no te T ero
Kare e tero e akairi ia ma ¯ri ua na roto i te ture.
69 Moni Koi’ia na te Katoatoa
Pouroa te au tero e tetai au moni e pera moni i koi ia me kore, tei rauka mai na
te Kavamani Kuki Airani, ka tutaki ia ki roto i te Akunı ¯ti a te Kavamani Kuki
Airani ma ¯ri ua me anoano ia me kore, akatika ia e te ture kia tutaki ia ki roto i
te akunı ¯ti a te katoatoa.
70 Akapou’anga
(1) Ko te au akapou’anga moni katoatoa mei roto i te Akunı ¯ti a te Kavamani o te
Kuki Airani me kore, tetai uatu akunı ¯ti a te iti tangata ka rave ia kia tau ki te
Ture Nui no te Akapapa’anga Moni ma ¯ri ua, me kua akatika ia me kore, tika ia
e tetai uatu ture.
(2) Ko tetai akataka’anga no te akapapa’anga moni no tetai akakoro’anga ua kia
oronga ia tetai akara anga no tetai au moni ka rauka mai no te reira
akakoro’anga e pera te moni i akapapa ia koia oki te moni ka toe mai.
(3) Na roto mai i te Minita o te Moni, tei na roto i te akatika anga a te Ka ¯pineti, me
kore, i te akataka anga a tetai ture, ka ariki atu te Konitara Aka’aere i te
akapou’anga o tetai moni tana i manako e kua tau—
(a) kia ariki atu i tetai akataka anga kia maani ia ki roto i te Ture Nui o te
Akapapa’anga Moni me kore, o tetai mataiti moni:
Mei te mea e akataka ia tetai akapou’anga moni e tei tutaki ia i roto i tetai
mataiti moni auraka i runga ake it e toenga o te moni i roto it e Ture Nui
no te Akapapa’anga moni (me kore au Ture Nui) no te mataiti moni o
mua atu e pera te maata o te moni tei aiteite atu ki te
toru-taingauru-ma-rua o te reira akapapa’anga moni; me kore
(b) i roto i te tuatau i pa ¯ti ia ei te Ture Nui no te Akapapa’anga Moni no tetai
mataiti moni e pera, i te openga o te reira mataiti ka anoano ia te reira
moni kia akapou ia tei vai ua me kore, kua pou ma te kore e
Akapapa’anga a te Paramani:
Kia tau oki e:
(i) ko te maata o te au moni ka oronga e ka tutaki ia auraka kia tere
atu i te 1.5% o te au moni i akapapa ia e te Ture Nui me kore au
Ture Nui no te Akapapa’anga Moni no te reira mataiti; e pera
(ii) no te reira ka rave atu te Kumiti o te Akarakara i te au
Akapou’anga Moni a te Katoatoa e ka oronga mai i te tamanako
anga ki te Minita o te Moni no te akaue atu i tetai tutaki anga moni
ki tetai uatu Tipatimani o te Kavamani me kore, Tuanga angaanga
a te Korona kia tau i raro ake i te paraka ¯va (b) kia tutaki iatu ki
Service 0123,401

roto i te Akunı ¯ti a te Kavamani Kuki Airani mei roto atu i te
akapapa’anga moni no te mataiti a muri ake.
[Atikara 70: mono ia, ra 1 July 1997, e te tuanga 2 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 22) Act
1997 (1997 No 17)..]
71 O ¯ tita
(1) Ko te Optai Otita o te Kuki Airani te o ¯ tita o te au Akunı ¯ti o te Kavamani Kuki
Airani e per ate tai atu au moni a te katoatoa me kore, au akunı ¯ti, e per ate au
akunı ¯ti a te au Tipatimani katoatoa e per ate au opati o te au aka’aere o te
kavamani e tetai atu au opati o te ture, me kore kavamani enua me kore taokotai
anga mei tei akataka ia e te ture.
(2) Ka rave atu te Opati o te O ¯tita, i te okotai taime i te mataiti, i te tuku atu ki te
V aa Tuatua o te Paramani i tetai ripoti no te au akapapa’anga tei anoano ia kia
tuku iatu e tetai ture, e pera te au akapapa’anga no runga i te Akunı ¯ti a te
Kavamani Kuki Airani me kore, tetai au akapapa’anga moni me kore, akunı ¯ti tei
akataka ia i roto i teia Papa Ture Metua me kore, tetai atu au ture tei anoano ia
kia o ¯ tita ia e te Opati o te O¯tita ta te reira Opati i manako e kia rave ia.
(3) Ka akatupu ia e te ture tetai Kumiti Akarakara i te Au Akapou’anga o te Moni
a te Katoatoa e ko te tama akatere i te reira koia oki na te Minita o te Moni e iki
mai, e pera katoa tetai au mema te ka akataka ia te maata anga e te turanga o to
ratou iki anga i roto i te Ture Nui.
(4) Ko te Ture Nui e taiku ia ra i roto i te iravaiti (3) o teia Atikara, ka akataka mai
ia ki te Kumiti Akarakara i te au Akapou’anga Moni a te Katoatoa i to ratou au
mana no te akarakara atu i te au akapou’anga moni mei roto atu i te Akunı ¯ti a
te Kavamani Kuki Airani e tetai atu au moni a te katoatoa, e pera tetai au tuanga
o te kavamani tei akataka ia e te ture, e ka rave katoa atu ratou i te au angaanga,
te au mana e te au angaanga i akataka ia e te ture.
[Atikara 71(1): akatuke’ia, ra 12 Aukute 1991, e te tuanga 4(1) o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’angat
(No 14) Act 1991 (1991 No 21).]
[Atikara 71(2): akatuke’ia, ra 5 Tiunu 1981, e te tuanga 6 e per ate Akapapa’anga 2 o te Papa Ture
Metua Akatuke’anga (No 9) Ture Nui 1980–81 (1980–81 No 24).]
[Atikara 71(3): mono ia, ra 11 Ma ¯ti 1996, e te tuanga 2 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 18)
Ture Nui 1995–96 (1995–96 No 8).]
[Atikara 71(4): mono ia, ra 11 Ma ¯ti 1996, e te tuanga 2 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 18)

Pae VI
T e Paepae Ropi’anga o te au T angata Angaanga a te Kavamani
[Pae VI: mono ia, ra 1 Tiurai 1995, e te tuanga 8 o te Papa Ture Akatuke’anga (No 17) Ture nui
1994–95 (1994–95 No 36).]
72 Paepae Ropi’anga o te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani
(1) Ka akatupu ia tetai Paepae Ropi’anga no te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani,
koia oki no te au tangata katoa e angaanga ra na te kavamani mei tetai taime ki
tetai tei akataka ia e te ture.
(2) Kua akataka mai te Ture i te akatere anga e pera te au ture iti no te Paepae
Ropi’anga angaanga ma te kore e akakotinga anga, i te iki anga, tuatau
angaanga, akatano anga, takore i te iki anga, e te akaoti i te au tangata angaanga
mei te angaanga, e tetai atu au akataka anga no te au tuanga angaanga tuketuke
a te kavamani.
73 Komitiona o te Paepae Ropi’anga o te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani
(1) Ka iki ia tetai Komitiona no te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani e te Kauono
o te Ariki V aine kia tau ki te akaue anga a te Parai Minita.
(2) Kare tetai tangata e akatika ia kia iki ia me kore, kia noo ua rai ei Komitiona no
te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani mei te mea e, me kore, me riro mai aia ei
Mema Paramani.
(3) Kare te Komitiona o te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani e akatika ia kia
angaanga no tetai opati ke ¯ atu o te Kavamani.
(4) Kare te au angaanga a te Komitiona o te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani e
takore ia no tetai au turanga taukore ka kitea mai mei roto i tona iki anga ia.
(5) Ka tutaki ia te Komitiona o te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani kit e moni
anganga e pera moni takake ¯ mei tetai taime ki tetai te ka akataka ia e te
Ka ¯pineti.
(6) Ko te akanoonoo anga ta te Komitiona o te au tangata angaanga ka a ¯ru no te
rave atu i tana au angaanga, e pera te oronga anga i tona au mana e te angaanga
kua akataka ia i roto i te ture.
74 T uatau e te au angaanga a te Komitiona o te Aronga Angaanga a te
Kavamani
(1) Ka iki ia te Komitiona o te Aronga Angaanga a te Kavamani e pera tona tuatau
angaanga e te Ka ¯pineti e ka iki akaou ia mei tetai taime ki tetai.
(2) Ka rauka i te Komitiona o te aronga angaanga a te Kavamani i te akaruke atu i
tana angaanga na roto i te ta ¯ta ¯ anga atu i tana peapa ki te Parai Minita i tetai uatu
taime.
(3) Na te Kauono o te Ariki V aine na roto it e akaue anga a te Parai Minita e ta ¯pu ¯
me kore akaa ¯tea it e Komitiona o te aronga angaanga mei te ngai angaanga no
te pakipakitai, pangikarapu, mako kore i te angaanga, aati i te au akanoonoo
anga no tona iki anga, me kore angaanga rave angaanga taukore.
(4) Ko te au angaanga a te Komitiona o te aronga angaanga a te Kavamani, kua
akataka ia i roto i te Ture.
75 Au T angata angaanga o te Kauono o te Ariki V aine
(1) T akake ¯ mei tei akataka ia i roto i e iravaiti (2) o teia Atikara, ko te iki anga,
Service 0123,601

tuatau angaanga, akatano anga, takore anga i te iki anga, e te kopae atu anga o
te au tangata angaanga o te Kauono o te Ariki V aine, ka vai rai te reira ki raro
ake i te mana o te Kauono o te Ariki V aine.
(2) Mei te mea e anoano te Kauono o te Ariki V aine, i te iki i tetai au tangata a te
Kavamani tana i inangaro kia angaanga nana na roto i tona mana, inara i muri
ake i te uriuri anga ki te Parai Minita, mei roto mai i te au ingoa ta te Komitiona
o te Paepae Ropianga angaanga a te Kavamani; e te au akataka’anga o te iravaiti
(1) o teia Atikara (ma ¯ri ua to ratou piri’anga ki te iki anga) ka iri atu ki runga
i tetai tangata tei iki ia no tona tuatau angaanga i roto i te au tangata angaanga
a te Kauono o te Ariki V aine e kare e no tona angaanga anga na te Paepae
Ropi’anga angaanga a te Kavamani.
76 Kopapa no te Apı ¯ra
(1) Ka akatupu ia tetai Kopapa Apı ¯ra no te Au T angata Angaanga o te Kavamani
koia oki ko—
(a) te Akavanui maata o te Akava’anga T eitei:
(b) okotai tangata, e tangata angaanga me kore, tangata angaanga kua ana na
te Kavamani Kuki Airani, ka iki ia, e ka angaanga tei ariki ia e te Kauono
o te Ariki V aine, tei rave ia mei tei akaue ia e te Parai Minita:
(c) okotai tangata, e tangata angaanga me kore, e tangata kua angaanga ana
na te Kavamani, ka iki ia mai e te au tangata angaanga a te Kavamani me
kore, tei nomineti ia e tetai taokotai anga o te reira au tangata angaanga,
e ka angaanga atu no tetai 3 mataiti.
(2) Ko te Akavanui maata te T ama Akatere o te Kopapa Apı ¯ra.
(3) Mei te mea e kare te Akavanui maata e tae ki tetai o te au uipaanga a te Kopapa
Apı ¯ra, ka riro e na tetai Akavanui o te Akava’anga T eitei tana i nomineti mai me
kore, no tetai akakoro’anga ke ¯, ka tomo mai ki roto i te uipaanga e koia katoa
te T ama Akatere o te Kopapa Apı ¯ra.
(4) Mei te mea e kare te Kavanui maata me kore, tetai Akavanui i nomineti ia e tae
atu mei tei akataka ia i raro ake i te iravaiti (3), ko te tangata i te reira tuatau e
mou ra i te taonga Akava Tutara Akamoeau, ka piri atu aia ki teia uipaanga e ka
riro atu ei T ama Akatere no te Kopapa Apı ¯ra.
(5) E Ture Nui—
(a) no te akataka mai i te turanga no te iki anga o tetai tangata i raro ake i te
au akataka’anga o te parakava (c) o te iravaiti (1) o teia Atikara e ka
akapeea tona iki anga me kore, nomineti anga:
(b) i te akataka mai i te iki anga o te au tangata tauturu kia riro ei mema no
te Kopapa Apı ¯ra tei iki ia i raro ake i te au akataka’anga o te parakava (b)
me kore parakava (c) o te iravaiti (1) o teia Atikara:
(c) te akataka mai i te mana o te Kopapa Apı ¯ra it e akarongo e te tuku i te tika
no te au apı ¯ra:
(d) no te akanoo i te akatere anga a te Kopapa Apı ¯ra.
(6) Kia tau ki te au akataka’anga o tetai Ture Nui, ka akanoo rai te Kopapa Apı ¯ra
i tana au akatere anga.
[The next page is 123,801]
Atikara 75LA WS OF THE COOK ISLANDS
Service 0 123,602

Pare VIA
Akataka’anga T akake
[Pae VIA: tauru ia, ra 5 Tiunu 1981, e te tuanga 13 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 9) Ture
Nui 1980–81 (1980–81 No 24).]
76A Au T angata ka oronga ia te tika’anga noo tinamou
(1) Ka rauka te tika’anga noo tinamou ki te Kuki Airani nei i tetai tangata mei te
mea e—
(a) kare te turanga o te reira tangatai i tau ki te turanga o te tangata Kuki
Airani no te tomo mai i raro ake i tetai uatu ture; e pera
(b) kua angai ia tetai tangata e tetai tangata Kuki Airani tei rauka te tika’anga
tomo mai i raro ake i tetai uatu ture; me kore
(c) kua angai ia tetai tangata i roto i te akono’anga tei ariki ia e te au ture o
te Kuki Airani; me korethe person is adopted in a manner recognised by
the laws of the Cook Islands; and
(d) i te tuatau o te angai anga, tei raro ake te mataiti o te reira tangata i te 18;
e pera
(e) kua pa ¯pu ¯ tikai te angai anga ia e kare i rave ia no te akakoro’anga kia
rauka te tika’anga noo tinamou ki konei.
(1A) Iravaiti (1B) ka iri ki tetai tangata tei—
(a) anau ia i mua ake i te mana anga o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No
29) Ture Nui 2021 (te Ture Nui Akatuke’anga 2021); e pera
(b) rauka te tika’anga noo tinamou i raro ake i te iravaiti (1) i mua ake i te
mana anga o te Ture Nui Akatuke’anga 2021.
(1B) Ko te tangata i akataka ia i roto i te iravaiti (1A) ka vai uatu rai tona tika’anga
noo tinamou.
(2) Ko tika ia tetai tangata kia tuku atu i tana pati’anga, kia tau ki te au akataka’anga
o tetai Ture Nui a te Paramani, no tetai tika’anga tika’anga noo tinamou ki te
Kuki Airani.
(3) Ka akamarama mai te Ture i te—
(a) i te au akataka anga no tetai tangata pati’anga i tetai tika’anga i raro ake
i te iravaiti (2) o teia Atikara, e te au turanga ka takore iatu te reira
tika’anga; e pera
(b) akataka katoa mai i te au turanga e oronga iatu ei te tika’anga ki tetai
tangata tei iri atu te iravaiti (2) o teia Atikara; e pera
(c) oronga i te mana ki te Minita kia oronga atu me kore, patoi atu i te oronga
i tetai tika’anga ki tetai tangata tei iri te iravaiti (2) o teia Atikara; e pera
(d) akataka mai i te turanga i oronga ia ei tetai tika’anga kia takore ia:
(e) akakite i te numero o te au akatika’anga no te au tangata noo tinamou no
te reira tuatau, tei oronga ia.
Akataka anga e ko tetai tika’anga i oronga ia, ka riro e na te Akavanui o te
Akava’anga T eitei e takore i te reira.
(4) T akake ¯ mei tetai o te au akataka’anga o teia Atikara, ka rauka i te Minita o te
Tuanga T omo’anga mai ki roto i te basileia i te takore atu i tetai tika’anga i
oronga ia ki tetai tangata mei te mea e, kua a ¯tea atu aia mei te Kuki Airani no
tetai tuatau roa tei tere atu i te 3 mataiti e na roto i te reira te akapapu mai e, kua
akamutu rai teia tangata i te akariro i te Kuki Airani ei ipukarea nona.
(5) Kare tetai tuanga i roto i teia Atikara e arapaki atu i te turanga noo tinamou o
Service 0123,801

tetai tangata i te Kuki Airani iaia e mou ra i te reira tika’anga i raro ake i te Ture
Nui T omo’anga, Noo’anga e te Akaruke’anga 1971-72, i mua ake i te mana anga
o teia Atikara.
[Atikara 76A(1): mono ia, ra 25 Noema 2021, e te tuanga 4 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No
29) Ture Nui 2021 (2021 No 8).]
[Atikara 76A(1A): tauru’ia, ra 25 Noema 2021, e te tuanga 4 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga

76B T e Tika’anga no te Aroa e te Akakore anga
Ko te Tika’anga no te Aroa e te Akakore’anga ka oronga ia te reira e te Kauono
o te Ariki V aine, kia tau ki te tika a te Paramani, koia oki ko te reira akakeu anga
kia turu ia e te au mema kare i raro ake i te rua-toru o te au mema (kapiti katoa
mai te au nooanga va ¯) o te Paramani.
[Atikara 76B: akatuke’ia, ra 6 Aperira 1982, e te tuanga 4(1) e pera te Akapapa’anga o te Papa Ture
Metua Akatuke’anga (No 10) Ture Nui 1981–82 (1981–82 No 20).]
76C T e Reva o te Kuki Airani
(1) Ko te Reva o te Kuki Airani koia oki te reva i akataka ia i roto i te Akapapa’anga
T oru o teia Papa Ture Metua.
(2) Ko te Reva o te Kuki Airani te akapa ¯pu ¯ ia nei ko te reva tei ariki ia no te Kuki
Airani.
(3) Ka maani ia tetai au akataka’anga na roto i te ture no te akataka mai i te au
turanga e te akanoonoo anga e tau ei kia uti ia te reva o te Kuki Airani ki runga,
e te arai anga atu i te reira na roto i te tuku anga i tetai akairo, akakite anga, me
kore reta ki reira.
76D Imene o te Basileia
(1) Ko te imene “T e Atua Mou E” ko te imene basileia te reira no te Kuki Airani.
(2) Ko te au tuatua o te imene basileia kua akapapa ia te reira i roto i te
Akapapa’anga A¯ o teia Papa Ture Metua.

Pae VII
Au T aui’anga
77 Au ture o teia ra kia ta’angaanga iatu rai
Kia tau ki te au akataka’anga o teia Papa Ture Metua—
(a) ko te au ture o teia ra, ma ¯ri ua me takore ia, e pera tetai uatu akatuke anga
katoa, ka mana uatu rai i te Ra Maata o te Kavamani e i muri ake i te
reira:
(b) ko te au tika’anga, apainga, e te au kaiou tei tupu mai mei roto it e au ture
o teia ra, ka vai rai te reira i mua ake e i muri katoa ake i te Ra Maata o
te Kavamani, e ka akara ia, rave ia e ka akatupu ia atu rai te reira.

81 Au T ure Akatere a te Konitara Maani T ure o Mua ana me kore Are Maani
T ure
(1) Ko te au Ture akatere tei maani ia e te Konitara Maani Ture o te Kuki Airani i
raro ake i te tuanga 2 o te Ture nui Akatuke’anga o te Kuki Airani 1946, te mana

te Konitara Maani ture o te Kuki Airani tei maani ia i mua ake i te Ra Maata o
te Kavamani e ka mana uatu rai mei te mea atura e au Ture Akatere no mua ake
e pera no muri ake i te Ra Maata o te Kavamani.

ake i te tuanga 38 o te Ture Nui Akatuke’anga o te Kuki Airani 1957, e te
ta’angaanga ia ra i mua ke i te Ra Maata o te Kavamani, ka mana uatu rai te reira
i mua e pera i muri ake i te Ra Maata o te Kavamani.
Service 0124,001

82 Akava’anga T eitei
(1) Ko te Akava’anga T eitei o te Kuki Airani tei akatupu ia e te Atikara 47 i teianei
koia katoa aia te Akava’anga T eitei o te Kuki Airani tei akatupu ia e te Ture Nui
o te Kuki Airani 1915.
(2) Ko te au Akavanui e te au Komitiona o te reira Akava’anga i mua ake i te Ra
Maata o te Kavamani, ka rave uatu rai i te angaanga mei ta ratou i matou i te
rave e pera i muri ake i te reira ra mei te mea atura e kua iki ia ratou ake i te au
akataka’anga o teia Papa Ture Metua, e ka tutaki ia te reira au Akavanui ra ki te
moni tutaki ta ratou e tutaki ia ana i mua ake i te Ra Maata o te Kavamani mei
te mea atura e kua akamana ia te reira e te ture.
(3) Ko te au akava’anga, tuku anga tika, rekoti, e te au ture no te Akava’anga T eitei
o te Kuki Airani ka mana uatu rai mei te tuatau i mua ake e pera i muri ake i te
Ra Maata o te Kavamani mei te mea atura e kua akamana ia i raro ake i teia
Papa Ture Metua; e ko te au akateretere anga katoatoa e pera te aronga ‘apa i te
ture e vai ra i mua i te Akava’anga T eitei i mua ake i te Ra Maata o te Kavamani
e pera te au apı ¯ra anga e vai ra i mua ake e i muri ake i te Ra Maata o te
Kavamani ka vai rai te reira.
83 Akava’anga Enua
(1) Ko te Akava’anga Enua o te Kuki Airani tei akatupu ia e te Atikara 52 koia
katoa rai te Akava’anga Tumu Enua o te Kuki Airani tei akatupu ia e te Ture Nui
o te Kuki Airani 1915.
(2) Ko te Akava’anga Enua o te Kuki Airani ka aite katoa tona au akakoro’anga mei
to te Akava’anga tei akatupu ia e te Ture Nui o te Kuki Airani 1915 tei kapiki
ia e ko te Akava’anga no te au Enua o te Kuki Airani e ko te au akaue anga tei
maani ia e te Akava’anga o mua atu ka mana rai te reira.
(3) [ T akore’ia]
[Atikara 83(3): takore’ia, ra 5 Tiunu 1981, e te tuanga 15 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No
9) Ture nui 1980–81 (1980–81 No 24).]

86 Akunı ¯ti a te Kavamani Kuki Airani
Ko te Akunı ¯ti a te Kavamani Kuki Airani tei akatupu ia e te Atikara 67 ko tei
kapiki katoa ia e ko te Akunı ¯ti a te T aokotai’anga o te Kuki Airani tei akatupu
ia e te tuanga 15 o te Ture nui Akatuke’anga o te Kuki Airani 1957; e ko te au
moni katoatoa i roto i te akunı ¯ti i taiku ia i mua akenei e, i mua katoa ake i te
Ra Maata o te Kuki Airani e i muri ake i te reira, e tuanga teia no te Akunı ¯ti a
te Kavamani Kuki Airani.

T uatau mou i te T aonga T ona Ngateitei Apenera Short OBE
Ko:
(1) T ona Ngateitei Apenera Short OBE tei mou i te taonga Kauono no te Ariki V aine
i te ra 19 o Titema 1990 e pera T ona Ngateitei te Ariki V aine tei Akaue i te iki
anga o T ona Ngateitei no tetai tuatau akaou tei kore i tupu vave e tae rava mai
ki te ra 11 o Okotopa 1994, ko tetai tuatau mei te 10 marama i muri ake i te pou
anga te tuatau angaanga mua o T ona Ngateitei.
(2) Ka karanga ia T ona Ngateitei e kua vai rai tona iki anga ia ei Kauono no te Ariki
V aine mei te ra 19 o Titema 1993 ki te ra 11 no Okotopa 1994 ma ¯ri ua, kare te
rua o te tuatau o T ona Ngateitei i akamata vave e tae rava mai ki te ra 11 o
Okotopa 1994 e ka ope i te ra 11 no Okotopa 1997.
(3) Ko te au angaanga opati pouroa tei rave ia e T ona Ngateitei mei te tuatau 19 o
Titema kit e ra 11 no Okotopa 1994 kua mana rai te reira mei te mea atura e kua
iki ia T ona Ngateitei ei Kauono no te Ariki V aine e T ona Ngateitei te Ariki V aine
it e reira tuatau.

(1997 No 3).]

T e au tuanga iki’anga o Aitutaki, Manuae, e T e-Au-O-T u

TUANGA IKI’ANGA O V AIP AE-T AUTU
Ko te au tuanga i runga i te Enua o Aitutaki tei ma ¯pu ia e tei akairo ia ki te peni muramura i
runga i te parani SO 1008 e vai ra i roto i te opati o te T angata Maata o te V aito Enua i Rarotonga,
koia ko—
(i) te T apere A vanui e tuanga no te Oire A vanui; e pera
(ii) te T apere Oako e te T apere V aipae o te Oire V aipae; e pera
(iii) te T apere Mataotane e te T apere T autu o te Oire T autu; e pera
(iv) te au motu koia ko—
Angarei
Niura
Mangere
Papau
T avairuaiti
T avairuanui
Akaiami
Muritapua
Rapota
Moturakau
T ekopua
T apuaetai
Motukitiu
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O AMURI-UREIA
Ko te au tuanga i runga i te Enua o Aitutaki tei ma ¯pu ia e tei akairo ia ki te peni auika i runga
i te parani SO 1008 e vai ra i roto i te opati o te T angata Maata o te V aito Enua i Rarotonga, koia
ko—
(i) te T apere Ureia e tuanga no te Oire Arutanga; e pera
(ii) te T apere Amuri e te T apere Punganu o te Oire Amuri; e pera
(iii) te T apere Anaunga e te T apere Punoua o te Oire Anaunga; e pera
(iv) te T apere T aakarere e te T apere V aitupa o te Oire V aitupa; e pera
(v) te T apere V aipeka, e tuanga no te Oire A vanui; e pera
(vi) te motu ko Akitua.

Pae II
Au T uanga iki’anga o te Enua Rarotonga e Pa ¯ mati
[Pae II: mono’ia, ra 11 Titema 1986, e te tuanga 3 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 12) Act 1986 (1986
No 19); akatuke’ia, ra 12 Aukute 1991, e te tuanga 3(3) e te (4) o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 14) Act
1991(1991 No 21).]

Ko te au tuanga enua i roto i te Oire A varua tei vaito ia i runga i te Enua Rarotonga koia oki te
T apere Pokoinu, Nikao, Puapuautu, Areanu, e Kaikaveka, tei ma ¯pu ia i runga i te parani SO 1002D
e vai ra i roto i te opati o te T angata Maata o te V aito Enua i Rarotonga.
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O A V A TIU-RUA TONGA
Ko te au tuanga enua i roto i te Oire A varua tei vaito ia i runga i te Enua Rarotonga koia oki te

o te T angata Maata o te V aito Enua i Rarotonga kapiti atu te Enua Pa ¯mati.
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O T AKUV AINE-TUT AKIMOA

T apere Tutakimoa, T auae, e T akuvaine, tei ma ¯pu ia i runga i te parani SO 1002D e vai ra i roto i te
opati o te T angata Maata o te V aito Enua i Rarotonga.
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O TUP AP A-MARAERENGA
Ko te au tuanga enua i roto i te Oire A varua tei vaito ia i runga i te Enua Rarotonga, koia oki te
T apere Ngatipa, V aikai, T apae-I-Uta, Pue, Punamaia, Kiikii e Tupapa tei ma ¯pu ia i runga i te parani
SO 1002D.
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O MA T A VERA
Ko te au tuanga enua i roto i te Oire Matavera tei vaito ia i runga i te Enua Rarotonga, tei ma ¯pu ia
i runga i te parani SO 1002D.
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O NGA T ANGIIA

TUANGA IKI’ANGA O TITIKA VEKA

Pae IV
Au T uanga iki’anga o te Enua Atiu
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O TENGA T ANGI-AREORA-NGA TIARUA
Ko te au tuanga i runga i te Enua Atiu tei koropini ia e te raini tei akamata i ko i te punanga Trig
CB1 e neke atu ki te tua opunga o te raini katau ki te tapa taatai ki te tukati anga raini ki te katau
i te vaito anga 45 tikiriti mei te CB1; neke atu ei ki te tua tonga-itinga a ¯ru atu ei i te raini ki te
akamata’anga, e te kapiti atu i te au tapere Areora, T engatangi, e Ngatiarua, tei ma ¯pu ia i runga i te
parani SO 1015 e vai ra i roto i te opati o te T angata Maata o te V aito Enua i Rarotonga.
TUANGA IKI’ANGA O TEENUI-MAPUMAI
Ko te au tuanga i runga i te Enua Atiu tei koropini ia e te raini tei akamata i ko i te punanga Trig
CB1 e neke atu ki te tua opunga o te raini katau ki te tapa taatai ki te tukati anga raini ki te katau
i te vaito anga 45 tikiriti mei te CB1; neke atu ei ki te tua tonga-itinga a ¯ru atu ei i te raini ki te
akamata’anga, e te kapiti atu i te au tapere T eenui e Mapumai, tei ma ¯pu ia i runga i te parani SO
1015.

T e Reva o te Kuki Airani
[Akapapa’anga T oru: tauru’ia, ra 5 Tiunu 1981, e te tuanga 16 e te Akapapa’anga 3 o te Papa Ture Metua
Akatuke’anga (No 9) Ture Nui 1980–81 (1980–81 No 24). ]
T eia te akama ¯rama anga i te Reva o te Kuki Airani i raro nei:
Ko te Reva o te Kuki Airani, ko te kara Ngateitei auika. Ko te akairo Union Jack tei te ko ¯ na i runga
i te tua kaui, e te au etu koropini e 15 aiteite te mamaata e te va ¯ i rotopu ia ratou, e te kara o te au
etu e teatea. ko te roa e te atea o te reva e rua e te tai.
Ko te aite’anga—
Auika — te kara rongonui o to tatou Basileia, koia oki te aite’anga no to tatou tuanga
tai Moana Patipika koropini ake i to tatou pa enua Kuki Airani. Ko te auika katoa e
akairo te reira no te natura ‘au o te iti tangata o to tatou pa enua.
Union Jack — e akairo te reira i to tatou piri’anga mei mua rava mai e mema no te ‘Au
Paratane.
T e 15 au etu teatea — e akairo teia no teo tatou au enua e 1.

Cook Islands Constitution Act 1964
T ABLE OF PROVISIONS
1 Short Title and Commencement
2 Interpretation and application
3 Cook Islands to be self-governing
4 Constitution of the Cook Islands
5 External af fairs and defence
6 British nationality and New Zealand citizenship
Schedule
Service 0129,101

[The next page is 129,201]
LA WS OF THE COOK ISLANDS
Service 0 129,102

An Act to make provision for self government by the people of the Cook Islands (other
than Niue) and to provide a constitution for those islands.
1 Short Title and Commencement
(1) This Act may be cited as the Cook Islands Constitution Act 1964.
(2) This Act shall come into force on a date to be appointed for the commencement
thereof by the Governor-General, by Proclamation, being a date later than the
date on which the ﬁrst meeting of the Legislative Assembly of the Cook Islands
is held after the ﬁrst general election of the Assembly held after the passing of
this Act.
[Section 1(2): amended, on 4 August 1965, by section 2(2) of the Cook Islands Constitution
Amendment Act (1965 No 2).]
2 Interpretation and application
(1) In this Act —
the Constitution means the Constitution of the Cook Islands as set out in the
Schedule to this Act
the Cook Islands has the same meaning as in the Constitution.
(2) This Act shall be in force in the Cook Islands and, unless the context otherwise
requires, shall apply to the Cook Islands only and not to New Zealand.
3 Cook Islands to be self-governing
The Cook Islands shall be self-governing.
4 Constitution of the Cook Islands
The Constitution set out in the Schedule to this Act shall be the Constitution of
the Cook Islands, and shall be the supreme law of the Cook Islands.
5 External af fairs and defence
Nothing in this Act or in the Constitution shall af fect the responsibilities of Her
Majesty the Queen in right of New Zealand for the external af fairs and defence
of the Cook Islands, those responsibilities to be discharged after consultation by
the Prime Minister of New Zealand with the Prime Minister of the Cook Islands.
[Section 5: amended, on 5 June 1981, by section 5 of the Constitution Amendment (No 9) Act
1980–81 (1980–81 No 24).]
6 British nationality and New Zealand citizenship
Nothing in this Act or in the Constitution shall af fect the status of any person as
a British subject or New Zealand citizen by virtue of the British Nationality and
New Zealand Citizenship Act 1948.
s 6 COOK ISLANDS CONSTITUTION ACT 1964

TEPERE AKAP AP A ’ANGA

Akapapa’anga
Service 0134,101

[The next page is 134,201]
LA WS OF THE COOK ISLANDS
Service 0 134,102

E Ture Nui no te maani i te akataka no te akatere anga i te kavamani o te iti tangata Kuki
Airani (takaka ¯ mei ia Niue) a te akataka katoa mai i tetai papa ture metua no te reira au
enua.
1 Upoko Poto e te Akamata’anga
(1) Ka kapiki ia teia Ture Nui e ko te Papa Ture Metua o te Kuki Airani Ture Nui
1964.
(2) Ka mana teia Ture Nui i te ra ka iki ia no te ta’angaanga i te reira e te
Kavana-Tianara, na roto i te Akakite’anga, i te ra i muri ake i te ra o te uipaanga
mua a te Are Maani Ture o te Kuki Airani i muri ake i te iki anga maata i rave
ia i muri ake i te pa ¯ti anga teia Ture Nui.
[Tuanga 1(2): akatuke’ia, ra 4 Aukute 1965, e te tuanga 2(2) o te Papa Ture Metua o te Kuki Airani
Akatuke’anga Ture Nui (1965 No 2).]
2 Aite’anga e te pirianga
(1) I roto i teia Ture Nui—
ko te Papa T ure Metua koia oki ko te Papa Ture Metua o te Kuki Airani tei
akataka ia i roto i te Akapapa’anga o teia Ture Nui
te Kuki Airani koia ko te aite’anga katoa i roto i te Papa Ture Metua.
(2) Ka mana teia Ture Nui i roto i te Kuki Airani e pera, me anoano ia no te
akakoro’anga, ka piri ki te Kuki Airani ua e kare a Nu Tireni.
3 T e Kuki Airani nana rai e akatere iaia uaorai
Na te Kuki Airani rai e akatere iaia uaorai.
4 Papa T ure Metua o te Kuki Airani
Kote Papa Ture Metua i akataka ia i roto i te Akapapa’anga o teia Ture Nui koia
te Papa Ture o te Kuki Airani, e ko te reira te ture tutara no te Kuki Airani.
5 Au angaanga i vao ake e te paruru
Kare tetai tuanga i roto i teia Ture Nui me kore, i roto i te Papa Ture Metua e
arapaki atu i te au angaanga a T ona Ngateitei te Ariki V aine na roto ia Nu Tireni
no te au angaanga i vao ake e pera te paruru anga i te Kuki Airani, ko te reira
au angaanga ka rave ia i muri ake i te uriuri anga manako i rotopu i te Parai
Minita o Nu Tireni ki te Parai Minita o te Kuki Airani.
[Tuanga 5: akatuke’ia, ra 5 Tiunu 1981, e te tuanga 5 o te Papa Ture Metua Akatuke’anga (No 9)
Ture Nui 1980–81 (1980–81 No 24).]
6 T angata Paratane e te Nu Tireni
Kare tetai tuanga i roto i teia Ture Nui me kore Papa Ture Metua e arapaki atu
i te turanga o tetai uatu tangata Paratane me kore Nu Tireni tei akataka ia e te
Ture Nui no te tangata Paratane e te T angata Nu Tireni 1948.

Elizabeth the Second, by the Grace of God Queen of New Zealand and Her Other Realms
and T erritories, Head of the Commonwealth, Defender of the Faith:
T o all to whom these presents shall come, Greeting:
Recites Letters Patent of 1 1 May 1917
Whereas by certain Letters Patent under the Great Seal of the United Kingdom bearing
date at W estminster the 11th day of May 1917, His late Majesty King George the Fifth
constituted, ordered, and declared that there should be a Governor-General and
Commander-in-Chief in and over the Dominion of New Zealand:
Recites Letters Patent of 18 December 1918
And whereas by certain Letters Patent under the Great Seal of the United Kingdom
bearing date at W estminster the 18th day of December 1918, His late Majesty King
George the Fifth made other provision for the publication and the coming into operation
of the said Letters Patent bearing date the 11th day of May 1917, in lieu of the provision
made in the Fifteenth Clause thereof:
Recites Royal Instructions of 1 1 May 1917
And whereas at the Court at St. James’s on the 11th day of May 1917, His late Majesty
King George the Fifth caused certain Instructions under the Royal Sign Manual and
Signet to be given to the Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief:
Recites Dormant Commission of 23 July 1917
And whereas at the Court at St. James’s on the 23rd day of July 1917, His late Majesty
King George the Fifth caused a Dormant Commission to be passed under the Royal Sign
Manual and Signet, appointing the Chief Justice or the Senior Judge for the time being of
the Supreme Court of New Zealand to administer the Government of New Zealand, in the
event of the death, incapacity , or absence of the Governor-General and
Commander-in-Chief and of the Lieutenant-Governor (if any):
Recites approval by Executive Council of draft of new Letters Patent
And whereas, by Order in Council bearing date at W ellington the 26th day of September
1983, Our Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief of New Zealand, acting by and
with the advice and consent of the Executive Council of New Zealand, has requested the
issue of new Letters Patent revoking and determining the said Letters Patent bearing date
the 11th day of May 1917, the said Letters Patent bearing date the 18th day of December
1918, the said Instructions, and the said Dormant Commission, and substituting in place
of the revoked documents other provision in the form of the draft of new Letters Patent
set out in Schedule 1 to that Order in Council:
Recites application of Letters Patent, Royal Instructions, and Dormant Commission to
Cook Islands and Niue
And whereas the said Letters Patent bearing date the 11th day of May 1917, the said
Letters Patent bearing date the 18th day of December 1918, the said Instructions, and the
said Dormant Commission extend to the self-governing state of the Cook Islands and to
the self-governing state of Niue as part of the law of the Cook Islands and of Niue,
respectively:
LETTERS P A TENT CONSTITUTING THE OFFICE OF GOVERNOR-GENERAL OF NZ 1983
Service 0139,201

Recites approval by Government of Cook Islands and Government of Niue of draft of new
Letters Patent
And whereas approval of the said draft of new Letters Patent has been signiﬁed on behalf
of the Government of the Cook Islands and the Government of Niue:
Ef fects revocations
Now , therefore, W e do by these presents revoke and determine the said Letters Patent
bearing date the 11th day of May 1917, the said Letters Patent bearing date the 18th day
of December 1918, the said Instructions, and the said Dormant Commission, but without
prejudice to anything lawfully done thereunder; and W e do hereby declare that the persons
who are members of the body known as the Executive Council of New Zealand
immediately before the coming into force of these Our Letters Patent shall be members of
Our Executive Council hereby constituted as though they had been appointed thereto
under these Our Letters Patent.
And W e do declare Our will and pleasure as follows:
1 Of fice of Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief constituted
W e do hereby constitute, order, and declare that there shall be, in and over Our
Realm of New Zealand, which comprises—
(a) New Zealand; and
(b) the self-governing state of the Cook Islands; and
(c) the self-governing state of Niue; and
(d) T okelau; and
(e) the Ross Dependency ,—
a Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief who shall be Our representative
in Our Realm of New Zealand, and shall have and may exercise the powers and
authorities conferred on him by these Our Letters Patent, but without prejudice
to the of f ice, powers, or authorities of any other person who has been or may be
appointed to represent Us in any part of Our Realm of New Zealand and to
exercise powers and authorities on Our behalf.
2 Appointment of Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief
And W e do hereby order and declare that Our Governor-General and
Commander-in-Chief (hereinafter called Our Governor-General) shall be
appointed by Us, by Commission under the Seal of New Zealand, and shall hold
of f ice during Our pleasure.
3 Governor-General’s powers and authorities
And W e do hereby authorise and empower Our Governor-General, except as
may be otherwise provided by law ,—
(a) to exercise on Our behalf the executive authority of Our Realm of New
Zealand, either directly or through of f icers subordinate to Our
Governor-General; and
(b) for greater certainty , but not so as to restrict the generality of the
foregoing provisions of this clause, to do and execute in like manner all
things that belong to the Of f ice of Governor-General including the
powers and authorities hereinafter conferred by these Our Letters Patent.
LA WS OF THE COOK ISLANDS
Service 0 139,202

4 Manner in which Governor-General’s powers and authorities are to be
executed
Our Governor-General shall do and execute all the powers and authorities of the
Governor-General according to—
(a) the tenor of these Our Letters Patent and of such Commission as may be
issued to Our Governor-General under the Seal of New Zealand; and
(b) such laws as are now or shall hereafter be in force in Our Realm of New
Zealand or in any part thereof.
5 Publication of Governor-General’s Commission
Every person appointed to ﬁll the Of f ice of Governor-General shall, before
entering on any of the duties of the of f ice, cause the Commission appointing him
to be Governor-General to be publicly read, in the presence of the Chief Justice,
or some other Judge of the High Court of New Zealand, and of members of the
Executive Council thereof.
6 Oaths to be taken by Governor-General
Our Governor-General shall, immediately after the public reading of the
Commission appointing him, take—
(a) the Oath of Allegiance in the form for the time being prescribed by the
law of New Zealand; and
(b) the Oath for the due execution of the Of f ice of Governor-General in the
form following:
I, [ name], swear that, as Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief of
the Realm of New Zealand, comprising New Zealand; the self-governing
states of the Cook Islands and Niue; T okelau; and the Ross Dependency ,
I will faithfully and impartially serve Her [ or His] Majesty [ specify the
name of the reigning Sovereign, as thus: Queen Elizabeth the Second],
Queen of New Zealand [or King of New Zealand], Her [or His] heirs and
successors, and the people of the Realm of New Zealand, in accordance
with their respective laws and customs. So help me God.
which Oaths the Chief Justice or other Judge in whose presence the Commission
is read is hereby required to administer.
[Clause 6(b): replaced, on 22 August 2006, by clause 1 of the Letters Patent (2006) Amending
Letters Patent Constituting the Of f ice of Governor-General of New Zealand. ]
7 Constitution of Executive Council
And W e do by these presents constitute an Executive Council to advise Us and
Our Governor-General in the Government of Our Realm of New Zealand.
8 Membership of Executive Council
The Executive Council shall consist of those persons who, having been
appointed to the Executive Council from among persons eligible for
appointment under the Constitution Act 1986, are for the time being Our
responsible advisers.
[Clause 8: replaced, on 1 January 1987, by clause 1 of the Letters Patent Amending Letters Patent
Constituting the Of f ice of Governor-General of New Zealand.]
9 Quorum of Executive Council
The Executive Council shall not proceed to the despatch of business unless two
members at the least (exclusive of any member presiding in the absence of Our
LETTERS P A TENT CONSTITUTING THE OFFICE OF GOVERNOR-GENERAL OF NZ 1983
Service 0139,203

Governor-General) be present throughout the whole of the meeting at which any
such business is despatched, except that in a situation of urgency or emergency ,
members may be present by any method of communication that allows each
member to participate ef fectively during the whole of the meeting.
[Clause 9: amended, on 22 August 2006, by clause 2 of the Letters Patent (2006) Amending Letters
Patent Constituting the Of f ice of Governor-General of New Zealand.]
10 Appointment of members of Executive Council, etc
And W e do hereby authorise and empower Our Governor-General, from time to
time in Our name and on Our behalf, to constitute and appoint under the Seal of
New Zealand, to hold of f ice during pleasure, all such members of the Executive
Council, Ministers of the Crown, commissioners, diplomatic or consular
representatives of New Zealand, principal representatives of New Zealand in
any other country or accredited to any international organisation, and other
necessary of f icers as may be lawfully constituted or appointed by Us.
11 Exercise of prerogative of mercy
And W e do further authorise and empower Our Governor-General, in Our name
and on Our behalf, to exercise the prerogative of mercy in Our Realm of New
Zealand, except in any part thereof where, under any law now or hereafter in
force, the prerogative of mercy may be exercised in Our name and on Our
behalf by any other person or persons, to the exclusion of Our
Governor-General; and for greater certainty but not so as to restrict the authority
hereby conferred, Our Governor-General may:
(a) grant, to any person concerned in the commission of any of fence for
which he may be tried in any court in New Zealand or in any other part
of Our said Realm to which this clause applies or to any person convicted
of any of fence in any such court, a pardon, either free or subject to lawful
conditions; or
(b) grant, to any person, a respite, either indeﬁnite or for a speciﬁed period,
of the execution of any sentence passed on that person in any court in
New Zealand or in any other part of Our said Realm to which this clause
applies; or
(c) remit, subject to such lawful conditions as he may think ﬁt to impose, the
whole or any part of any such sentence or of any penalty or forfeiture
otherwise due to Us on account of any of fence in respect of which a
person has been convicted by any court in New Zealand or in any other
part of Our said Realm to which this clause applies.
12 Administrator of the Government
Whenever the Of f ice of Governor-General is vacant, or the holder of the Of f ice
is for any reason unable to perform all or any of the functions of the Of f ice, W e
do hereby authorise, empower, and command the Chief Justice of New Zealand
to perform the functions of the Of f ice of Governor-General. If, however, there is
for the time being no Chief Justice able to act as Governor-General, then the
next most senior Judge of the New Zealand judiciary who is able so to act is so
authorised, empowered, and commanded. The Chief Justice or the next most
senior Judge, while performing all or any of the functions of the Of f ice of
Governor-General, is to be known as the Administrator of the Government; and
LA WS OF THE COOK ISLANDS
Service 0 139,204

in these Our Letters Patent every reference to Our Governor-General includes,
unless inconsistent with the context, a reference to Our Administrator of the
Government.
[Clause 12: replaced, on 22 August 2006, by clause 3 of the Letters Patent (2006) Amending Letters
Patent Constituting the Of f ice of Governor-General of New Zealand.]
13 Oaths to be taken by Administrator of the Government
The said Chief Justice or next most senior Judge of the New Zealand judiciary
shall, on the ﬁrst occasion on which he is required to act as Administrator of the
Government and before entering on any of the duties of the Of f ice of
Governor-General, take the Oaths hereinbefore directed to be taken by Our
Governor-General, which Oaths, with such modiﬁcations as are necessary , shall
be administered by some other Judge of the High Court of New Zealand, in the
presence of not less than two members of the Executive Council.
[Clause 13: replaced, on 22 August 2006, by clause 4 of the Letters Patent (2006) Amending Letters
Patent Constituting the Of f ice of Governor-General of New Zealand.]
14 Powers and authorities of Governor-General not abridged
While Our Administrator of the Government is performing all or any of the
functions of the Of f ice of Governor-General, the powers and authorities of Our
Governor-General shall not be abridged, altered, or in any way af fected,
otherwise than as W e may at any time hereafter think proper to direct.
15 Governor-General’s absence
[Revoked]
[Clause 15: revoked, on 22 August 2006, by clause 5 of the Letters Patent (2006) Amending Letters
Patent Constituting the Of f ice of Governor-General of New Zealand.]
16 Ministers to keep Governor-General informed
Our Ministers of the Crown in New Zealand shall keep Our Governor-General
fully informed concerning the general conduct of the Government of Our said
Realm, so far as they are responsible therefor, and shall furnish Our
Governor-General with such information as he may request with respect to any
particular matter relating to the Government of Our said Realm.
17 Ministers and others to obey, aid, and assist Governor-General
Our Ministers of the Crown and other of f icers, civil and military , and all other
inhabitants of Our Realm of New Zealand, shall obey , aid, and assist Our
Governor-General in the performance of the functions of the Of f ice of
Governor-General.
18 Power reserved to Her Majesty to revoke, alter , or amend the present
Letters Patent
And W e do hereby reserve to Ourselves, Our heirs and successors, full power
and authority from time to time to revoke, alter, or amend these Our Letters
Patent as to Us or them shall seem meet.
19 Present Letters Patent to have ef fect as law
And W e do further declare that these Our Letters Patent shall take ef fect as part
of the law of Our Realm of New Zealand, comprising New Zealand, the
LETTERS P A TENT CONSTITUTING THE OFFICE OF GOVERNOR-GENERAL OF NZ 1983
Service 0139,205

self-governing state of the Cook Islands, the self-governing state of Niue,
T okelau, and the Ross Dependency on the 1st day of November 1983.
In witness whereof W e have caused these Our Letters to be made Patent, and for
the greater testimony and validity thereof W e have caused the Seal of New
Zealand to be af f ixed to these presents, which W e have signed with Our Regal
Hand.
Given the 28th day of October in the Y ear of Our Lord One Thousand Nine
Hundred and Eighty-three and in the 32nd Y ear of Our Reign.
